        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





Need certain times of iteration, May crash at second group or 99th group



<span class="line"><!---->Need certain times of iteration, May crash at second group or 99th group<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: stable



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: stable<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: All



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: All<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Install the attached extension.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Install the attached extension.<!----></span>



<br>





2. It will crash in several times of iteration.



<span class="line"><!---->2. It will crash in several times of iteration.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION



<b class="line"><!---->FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>





Type of crash: browser



<span class="line"><!---->Type of crash: browser<!----></span>



<br>





Crash State: see attached file



<span class="line"><!---->Crash State: see attached file<!----></span>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





a8728eead1b427868420b003180f17a85e88554b



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/a8728eead1b427868420b003180f17a85e88554b"><!---->a8728eead1b427868420b003180f17a85e88554b<!----></a>

Author: Connie Wan <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Connie Wan &lt;<!----></span>





connily@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/connily@chromium.org"><!---->connily@chromium.org<!----></a>

<br>





Date: Thu Jan 07 22:05:27 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Thu Jan 07 22:05:27 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Make grouping and pinning cause less tab movement



<span class="line"><!---->Make grouping and pinning cause less tab movement<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Grouping was originally causing two tab movements: one to unpin the tab,



<span class="line"><!---->Grouping was originally causing two tab movements: one to unpin the tab,<!----></span>



<br>





then another to group. Reducing this to a single movement reduces the



<span class="line"><!---->then another to group. Reducing this to a single movement reduces the<!----></span>



<br>





potential for race conditions when rapidly pinning and grouping/unpinning



<span class="line"><!---->potential for race conditions when rapidly pinning and grouping/unpinning<!----></span>



<br>





tabs.



<span class="line"><!---->tabs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tested manually and via existing unit tests:



<span class="line"><!---->Tested manually and via existing unit tests:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/tabs/tab_strip_model_unittest.cc;l=3175



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/tabs/tab_strip_model_unittest.cc;l=3175"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/tabs/tab_strip_model_unittest.cc;l=3175<!----></a>



<br>



<br>

Thanks for this report! I believe the change I just made should address this particular issue in MoveWebContents from the conflict of pinning vs. grouping.



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for this report! I believe the change I just made should address this particular issue in MoveWebContents from the conflict of pinning vs. grouping.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





However, I haven't been able to test the repro directly because loading infinite-looping extensions in a test understandably causes other issues.



<span class="line"><!---->However, I haven't been able to test the repro directly because loading infinite-looping extensions in a test understandably causes other issues.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The change should be available with the next Canary, so I may be able to test more then to verify a fix.



<span class="line"><!---->The change should be available with the next Canary, so I may be able to test more then to verify a fix.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Jan 27 20:53:18 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Make grouping and pinning cause less tab movement (merge)



<span class="line"><!---->Make grouping and pinning cause less tab movement (merge)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Grouping was originally causing two tab movements: one to unpin the tab,



<span class="line"><!---->Grouping was originally causing two tab movements: one to unpin the tab,<!----></span>



<br>





then another to group. Reducing this to a single movement reduces the



<span class="line"><!---->then another to group. Reducing this to a single movement reduces the<!----></span>



<br>





potential for race conditions when rapidly pinning and grouping/unpinning



<span class="line"><!---->potential for race conditions when rapidly pinning and grouping/unpinning<!----></span>



<br>





tabs.



<span class="line"><!---->tabs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tested manually and via existing unit tests:



<span class="line"><!---->Tested manually and via existing unit tests:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/tabs/tab_strip_model_unittest.cc;l=3175



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/tabs/tab_strip_model_unittest.cc;l=3175"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:chrome/browser/ui/tabs/tab_strip_model_unittest.cc;l=3175<!----></a>



<br>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
